Author-defined elements

[phrasing](dom.html#phrasing-content-2){#elements-3:phrasing-content-2-149};

[phrasing](dom.html#phrasing-content-2){#elements-3:phrasing-content-2-150}

[transparent](dom.html#transparent){#elements-3:transparent-10}

[globals](dom.html#global-attributes){#elements-3:global-attributes-108};
any, as decided by the element\'s author

Supplied by the element\'s author (inherits from
[`HTMLElement`{#elements-3:htmlelement-40}](dom.html#htmlelement))

[An asterisk (\*) in a cell indicates that the actual rules are more
complicated than indicated in the table above.]{.small}

[â€  Categories in the \"Parents\" column refer to parents that list the
given categories in their content model, not to elements that themselves
are in those categories. For example, the
[`a`{#elements-3:the-a-element-2}](text-level-semantics.html#the-a-element)
element\'s \"Parents\" column says \"phrasing\", so any element whose
content model contains the \"phrasing\" category could be a parent of an
[`a`{#elements-3:the-a-element-3}](text-level-semantics.html#the-a-element)
element. Since the \"flow\" category includes all the \"phrasing\"
elements, that means the
[`th`{#elements-3:the-th-element-3}](tables.html#the-th-element) element
could be a parent to an
[`a`{#elements-3:the-a-element-4}](text-level-semantics.html#the-a-element)
element.]{.small}

state);

[`li`{#element-content-categories:the-li-element-3}](grouping-content.html#the-li-element)
element);

that is not [inter-element
whitespace](dom.html#inter-element-whitespace){#element-content-categories:inter-element-whitespace}

### Attributes[](#attributes-3){.self-link} {#attributes-3 .no-num}

*This section is non-normative.*

List of attributes (excluding event handler content attributes)

Attribute

Element(s)

Description

Value

`abbr`

[`th`{#attributes-3:attr-th-abbr}](tables.html#attr-th-abbr)

Alternative label to use for the header cell when referencing the cell
in other contexts

[Text](dom.html#attribute-text)\*

`accept`

[`input`{#attributes-3:attr-input-accept}](input.html#attr-input-accept)

Hint for expected file type in [file upload
controls](input.html#file-upload-state-(type=file)){#attributes-3:file-upload-state-(type=file)}

[Set of comma-separated
tokens](common-microsyntaxes.html#set-of-comma-separated-tokens){#attributes-3:set-of-comma-separated-tokens}\*
consisting of [valid MIME type strings with no
parameters](https://mimesniff.spec.whatwg.org/#valid-mime-type-with-no-parameters){#attributes-3:valid-mime-type-string-with-no-parameters
x-internal="valid-mime-type-string-with-no-parameters"} or `audio/*`,
`video/*`, or `image/*`

`accept-charset`

[`form`{#attributes-3:attr-form-accept-charset}](forms.html#attr-form-accept-charset)

Character encodings to use for [form
submission](form-control-infrastructure.html#form-submission-2){#attributes-3:form-submission-2}

[ASCII
case-insensitive](https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#ascii-case-insensitive){#attributes-3:ascii-case-insensitive
x-internal="ascii-case-insensitive"} match for \"`UTF-8`\"

`accesskey`

[HTML
elements](interaction.html#the-accesskey-attribute){#attributes-3:the-accesskey-attribute}

Keyboard shortcut to activate or focus element

[Ordered set of unique space-separated
tokens](common-microsyntaxes.html#ordered-set-of-unique-space-separated-tokens){#attributes-3:ordered-set-of-unique-space-separated-tokens},
none of which are [identical
to](https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#string-is){#attributes-3:identical-to
x-internal="identical-to"} another, each consisting of one code point in
length

`action`

[`form`{#attributes-3:attr-fs-action}](form-control-infrastructure.html#attr-fs-action)

[URL](https://url.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-url){#attributes-3:url
x-internal="url"} to use for [form
submission](form-control-infrastructure.html#form-submission-2){#attributes-3:form-submission-2-2}

[Valid non-empty URL potentially surrounded by
spaces](urls-and-fetching.html#valid-non-empty-url-potentially-surrounded-by-spaces){#attributes-3:valid-non-empty-url-potentially-surrounded-by-spaces}

`allow`

[`iframe`{#attributes-3:attr-iframe-allow}](iframe-embed-object.html#attr-iframe-allow)

[Permissions
policy](https://w3c.github.io/webappsec-feature-policy/#permissions-policy){#attributes-3:concept-permissions-policy
x-internal="concept-permissions-policy"} to be applied to the
[`iframe`{#attributes-3:the-iframe-element}](iframe-embed-object.html#the-iframe-element)\'s
contents

[Serialized permissions
policy](https://w3c.github.io/webappsec-feature-policy/#serialized-permissions-policy){#attributes-3:concept-serialized-permissions-policy
x-internal="concept-serialized-permissions-policy"}

`allowfullscreen`

[`iframe`{#attributes-3:attr-iframe-allowfullscreen}](iframe-embed-object.html#attr-iframe-allowfullscreen)

Whether to allow the
[`iframe`{#attributes-3:the-iframe-element-2}](iframe-embed-object.html#the-iframe-element)\'s
contents to use
[`requestFullscreen()`{#attributes-3:dom-element-requestfullscreen}](https://fullscreen.spec.whatwg.org/#dom-element-requestfullscreen){x-internal="dom-element-requestfullscreen"}

[Boolean
attribute](common-microsyntaxes.html#boolean-attribute){#attributes-3:boolean-attribute}

`alpha`

[`input`{#attributes-3:attr-input-alpha}](input.html#attr-input-alpha)

Allow the color\'s alpha component to be set

[Boolean
attribute](common-microsyntaxes.html#boolean-attribute){#attributes-3:boolean-attribute-2}

`alt`

[`area`{#attributes-3:attr-area-alt}](image-maps.html#attr-area-alt);

[Text](dom.html#attribute-text)\*

`as`

[`link`{#attributes-3:attr-link-as}](semantics.html#attr-link-as)

destination](https://fetch.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-potential-destination){#attributes-3:concept-potential-destination
x-internal="concept-potential-destination"} for a preload request (for
[`rel`{#attributes-3:attr-link-rel}](semantics.html#attr-link-rel)=\"[`preload`{#attributes-3:link-type-preload}](links.html#link-type-preload)\"
and
[`rel`{#attributes-3:attr-link-rel-2}](semantics.html#attr-link-rel)=\"[`modulepreload`{#attributes-3:link-type-modulepreload}](links.html#link-type-modulepreload)\")

[Potential
destination](https://fetch.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-potential-destination){#attributes-3:concept-potential-destination-2
x-internal="concept-potential-destination"}, for
[`rel`{#attributes-3:attr-link-rel-3}](semantics.html#attr-link-rel)=\"[`preload`{#attributes-3:link-type-preload-2}](links.html#link-type-preload)\";
[script-like
destination](https://fetch.spec.whatwg.org/#request-destination-script-like){#attributes-3:concept-script-like-destination

[`rel`{#attributes-3:attr-link-rel-4}](semantics.html#attr-link-rel)=\"[`modulepreload`{#attributes-3:link-type-modulepreload-2}](links.html#link-type-modulepreload)\"

### Events[](#events-2){.self-link} {#events-2 .no-num}

*This section is non-normative.*

The following table lists events fired by this document, excluding those
already defined in [media element events](media.html#mediaevents) and
[drag-and-drop events](dnd.html#dndevents).

its [activation
behavior](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#eventtarget-activation-behavior){#events-2:activation-behaviour

from a non-pointer input device (e.g. a keyboard)

[`Event`{#events-2:event-12}](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event){x-internal="event"}

Global scope objects, [`Worker`{#events-2:worker}](workers.html#worker)
objects, elements, networking-related objects

Fired when unexpected errors occur (e.g. networking errors, script
errors, decoding errors)

as a result of a navigation.

### HTTP headers[](#http-headers){.self-link} {#http-headers .no-num}

*This section is non-normative.*

The following HTTP request headers are defined by this specification:

- \`[`Last-Event-ID`{#http-headers:last-event-id}](server-sent-events.html#last-event-id)\`
- \`[`Ping-From`{#http-headers:ping-from}](links.html#ping-from)\`
- \`[`Ping-To`{#http-headers:ping-to}](links.html#ping-to)\`

The following HTTP response headers are defined by this specification:

- \`[`Cross-Origin-Embedder-Policy`{#http-headers:cross-origin-embedder-policy}](browsers.html#cross-origin-embedder-policy)\`
- \`[`Cross-Origin-Embedder-Policy-Report-Only`{#http-headers:cross-origin-embedder-policy-report-only}](browsers.html#cross-origin-embedder-policy-report-only)\`
- \`[`Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy`{#http-headers:cross-origin-opener-policy-2}](browsers.html#cross-origin-opener-policy-2)\`
- \`[`Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy-Report-Only`{#http-headers:cross-origin-opener-policy-report-only}](browsers.html#cross-origin-opener-policy-report-only)\`
- \`[`Origin-Agent-Cluster`{#http-headers:origin-agent-cluster}](browsers.html#origin-agent-cluster)\`
- \`[`Refresh`{#http-headers:refresh}](document-lifecycle.html#refresh)\`
- \`[`X-Frame-Options`{#http-headers:x-frame-options}](document-lifecycle.html#x-frame-options)\`

### MIME types[](#mime-types-2){.self-link} {#mime-types-2 .no-num}

*This section is non-normative.*

The following MIME types are mentioned in this specification:

[`application/atom+xml`]{#application/atom+xml .dfn}
:   Atom [\[ATOM\]](references.html#refsATOM)

[`application/json`]{#application/json .dfn}
:   JSON [\[JSON\]](references.html#refsJSON)

[[`application/octet-stream`](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2046#section-4.5.1)]{#application/octet-stream .dfn}
:   Generic binary data [\[RFC2046\]](references.html#refsRFC2046)

[`application/microdata+json`{#mime-types-2:application/microdata+json}](iana.html#application/microdata+json)
:   Microdata as JSON

[`application/rss+xml`]{#application/rss+xml .dfn}
:   RSS

[`application/wasm`]{#application/wasm .dfn}
:   WebAssembly [\[WASM\]](references.html#refsWASM)

[`application/x-www-form-urlencoded`{#mime-types-2:application/x-www-form-urlencoded}](https://url.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-urlencoded){x-internal="application/x-www-form-urlencoded"}
:   Form submission

[`application/xhtml+xml`{#mime-types-2:application/xhtml+xml}](iana.html#application/xhtml+xml)
:   HTML

[`application/xml`]{#application/xml .dfn}
:   XML [\[XML\]](references.html#refsXML)
    [\[RFC7303\]](references.html#refsRFC7303)

[`image/gif`]{#image/gif .dfn}
:   GIF images [\[GIF\]](references.html#refsGIF)

[`image/jpeg`]{#image/jpeg .dfn}
:   JPEG images [\[JPEG\]](references.html#refsJPEG)

[`image/png`]{#image/png .dfn}
:   PNG images [\[PNG\]](references.html#refsPNG)

[`image/svg+xml`]{#image/svg+xml .dfn}
:   SVG images [\[SVG\]](references.html#refsSVG)

[`multipart/form-data`]{#multipart/form-data .dfn}
:   Form submission [\[RFC7578\]](references.html#refsRFC7578)

[`multipart/mixed`]{#multipart/mixed .dfn}
:   Generic mixed content [\[RFC2046\]](references.html#refsRFC2046)

[`multipart/x-mixed-replace`{#mime-types-2:multipart/x-mixed-replace}](iana.html#multipart/x-mixed-replace)
:   Streaming server push

[`text/css`]{#text/css .dfn}
:   CSS [\[CSS\]](references.html#refsCSS)

[`text/event-stream`{#mime-types-2:text/event-stream}](iana.html#text/event-stream)
:   Server-sent event streams

[`text/javascript`]{#text/javascript .dfn}
:   JavaScript [\[JAVASCRIPT\]](references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)
    [\[RFC9239\]](references.html#refsRFC9239)

[`text/json`]{#text/json .dfn}
:   JSON (legacy type)

[[`text/plain`](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc2046#section-4.1.3)]{#text/plain .dfn}
:   Generic plain text [\[RFC2046\]](references.html#refsRFC2046)
    [\[RFC3676\]](references.html#refsRFC3676)
